 Today is the birth anniversary of Mirza Ghalib, one of the strongest signatures of Urdu
 
 
 puraani dilli ke balli maaraan ilaake kii gali kasim jaan main rahane vaale asadulla khan gaalib ko duniya aaj tak mirza gaalib ke naam se yaad karti he, or ham maukey par unke kahe sher hi logon ko yaad aate hai
 
 
 Recently, Congress Vice President Rahul Gandhi had also read Mirza Ghalib's lion while taking a sarcasm at Prime Minister Narendra Modi regarding demonetisation
 
 
 27 disambar, 1797 ko uttar pradesh ke agra main ek sainik prishthbhumi vaale parivaar main janme mirza gaalib ne hazaron sher kahe, jinhen bhula paanaa kisi ke liye bhi aasaan nahin he
 
 
 Mirza Ghalib is said to have lived only through the pension of his uncle, who was a military officer in the East India Company, who was very young, so he lived in Tumr Qilat, and died on 15 February 1869
 
 
 bahut choti umr, yani 12 saal kii umr se hi urdu or farsi main likhnaa shuru kar dene vaale mirza gaalib ke 10 sher ham aaj aapke saamne pesh kar rahe hai, jo behad mashhoor rahe hai

 ishk, aashiq or mashooq hameshaa se urdu shaayari main shumaar rahe hai, so, mirza gaalib bhi ishk ko chhodkar nahin rah sakate the -ye ishk nahin asaan, itnaa hi samaj lijai, Ik is a river of fire, and has to be drowned

 Terrorists attacked grenade at Jammu bus stand in March
 Bus stand in Jammu has been a target of terrorists earlier and security forces today on Tuesday Nearly 15 kg of explosives were recovered from a bus near Jammu bus stand and foiled a major terror conspiracy
 yah bag kathua jile ke bilawar tehsil se aa rahaa tha
 The bag was given to the conductor of the bus
 philhal suraksha balon ne visphotakon ko baraamad kar liya he
 It is now being investigated after a large quantity of explosives were recovered
 ek sandigdh ko hiraasat main liya gaya he or usase poochtacha kii ja rahi he
 The security forces stopped the bus near Jammu bus stand after receiving information about suspicious goods in the bus and it was investigated
 jaanch main visphotakon se bharaa bag baraamad hua
 a suspect is being apprehended and questioned
 kab lagegi lagaam?isse pehle bhi jammu bas stand par aatanki apana sajeesh ko anjaam dete rahe hai
 On March 7 this year, terrorists attacked the Jammu bus stand with a grenade
 is hamale main 2 logon kii maut ho gai jabaki 30 se zyada log ghayal ho gaye the
 Then Jammu and Kashmir Governor Satyapal Malik had announced a grant of Rs
 5 lakh each to the close relatives of the deceased and Rs
 20,000 to each injured
 narendra modi ke pradhanmantri banane ke baad rashtriya swayamsevak sangh or usase jude sanghathanon kii buudhvaar ko dilli main shuru hui pehali teen divasiy samanvay baithak main sangh, sarkaar or bhaajapa ke varisht logon ne vibhinn rashtriya muddon par charchaa kii
 It is being told that in this meeting, many ministers of the government also kept the details of the functioning of their ministries
 sangh ne apni chintaaon se sarkaar ke varisht mantriyon ko bhi avgat karaayaa
 It is said that in the meeting, the issue of ex-servicemen movement on Jantar Mantar demanding forest rank, forest pension also came up and the union officials believe that the prolongation of the movement of ex-servicemen can affect the image of the government
 And it should be resolved as soon as possible
 bhaajapa mahasachiv ram madhav ne haalanki kaha ki baithak ke dauraan kuch samasamyik vishay jarur uthe, lekin yah vishay nahin aayaa
 He said that this is a policy issue on which the government is moving forward
 baithak main arun jetali, sushamaa swaraj, rajnath singh, manohar parrikar, venkaiya naidu, anant kumaar or bhaajapa adhyaksh amit shah ne bhi hissaa liya
 Prime Minister Narendra Modi is expected to attend the last day of the meeting
 aresas ke pramukh mohan bhagwat kii adhyakshata main ho rahi is samanvay baithak main sarkaar ke kaam kaaj ke bare main charchaa hone kii khabaron par sutron ne kaha ki yah sarkaar ke bahikhaate kii baithak nahin he balki isamen sangh se jude vibhinn sanghathan masalan seva bharti, vidya bharti, vanavaasi kalyaan, vishwa hindu parishad, vidhyaarthee parishad aadi ne saal bhar main kya kiya or aage kya karenge, us par prastuti di jaati he
 The source said that this time the meeting has taken a slightly different form because a lot of incidents are happening in the society
 desh bhar main saal bhar gum-gum kar janata ke soch kaa jayja lene vaale sangh ke akhil bhartiya padaadhikariyon se inke bare main vyapak input mili hai

 Gold is ready to shine in this Diwali
 bazaar ke vishleshkon kaa maananaa he ki yah dhanteras tak 33,000 rupee prati das gram tak chalaa jayega
 This uptick in gold prices will be due to lack of this yellow metal in the market and due to festivals
 sone ke aayaat ko ghataane kii sarkari koshishon kaa parinaam yah hua he ki sone ke stock main kami ai he
 India is the world's largest buyer of gold and imports the most
 is kaaran sarkaar kaa bajet ghaataa lagaataar badhata ja rahaa tha or yah chintajanak str par ja pahunchaa he
 To prevent this, the government has enacted stringent laws, which have reduced its revenue
 pichhali timahi main sone kaa aayaat sirf 59 ton hi hua, jabaki uske pehle kii timahi main yah 335 ton tha
 There is a shortage of stock due to this steep decline
 kaarobaariyon kaa maananaa he ki sone ke stock main kami ke kaaran yah or upar jayega
 The general secretary of the Bullion Merchants Association, Shri Krishna Goyal Chandiwala said that the price of gold has increased due to the decrease in the stock
 haalat yah he ki sone is samay emsiex kii keemton se 1,500 rupee prati das gram tak zyada he
 Due to lack of stock and festivals, its prices can go up and if it crosses Rs 33,000 per ten grams, then there should be no surprise
 anya kaarobaariyon kaa bhi maananaa he ki tyohaaron ke kaaran sone ke daam thode upar ja sakate hai
 But Goyal believes that gold prices will also fall after Diwali as it is not at the actual level
 sabsidi vaale gharelu rasoi gas silendar kaa daam somvaar ko do rupee prati silendar badha diya gaya, jabaki rashan main bikne vaala mitti tel 26 paise litre mahangaa hua he
 The government is moving forward on the plan to end the subsidy on these fuels by increasing the price of these fuels a little
 dilli main gharelu rasoi gas silendar kaa daam 1
 Rs 87 per cylinder increased to 442
 77 rupee prati silendar kar diya gaya
 Public sector petroleum companies have given this information
 tel companiyon ne isse pehle 1 april ko sabsidishuda gas silendar kaa daam 5
 57 by Rs
 440
 90 rupee prati (14

 When new teachers, who are getting training from the state government, arrive late in class, in some places they are welcomed with loud applause
 darasal, pradesh main TET paas shikshakon kii bade paimaane par bhartee hui he, jinhen group main 30-30 dinon kii special training (prerana-2) di jaati he
 The center where such training is imparted is called BRC (block Resource Center)
 sabhi shikshakon ko training ke liye tay vakt par pahunchnaa hota he
 When a teacher who is training arrives late in class, the other teachers welcome them with applause
 aisi taaliyon ko yahaan ‘teen tali’ kaha jaataa he
 The purpose of playing such claps is that the late visitor realizes that he has made a mistake by not coming on time
 saath hi galatiyon kaa ehsaas is tareeke se karaayaa jaae ki kisi ke man main thes bhi na pahunche
 Coordinator Madhurendra Kumar 'madhup' of Cluster Resource Center, Kanyar Middle School, Maner, said, "usually after the end of lunch time, there are constant applause for the teachers outside the room to call in
 , Upon hearing which they immediately return
 let aane par taaliyaan bajaae jane kaa chalan har jagah nahin he
 He said that at the end of lunch, such applause is played instead of bell
 saath hi training ke dauraan kisi kii khaas uplabdhi par yaa centre par kisi behad khaas guest ke aane par 'paanch taaliyon' se unka swaagat hota he
 All such applause is called clap of BEP (bihar Education Project)
 ek or dilachasp baat yah he ki agar samuhik rup se taaliyaan bajaane ke kram main koi lay khokar galati kar baithta he, to use ‘bonus’ ke taur par sabhi ko geet, latifa yaa koi prerak prasang sunaanaa padataa he
 Latecomers are similarly 'punished'

 If the teacher himself is late, what will the children learn from him? ’ unhone kaha ki let aane par jis tarah kaa ‘swaagat’ hota he, usase kisi ko bura bhi nahin lagata he or galati karne vaale tak taaliyon se hi ‘massej’ bhi pahunch jaataa he

 padmashri:bharat ke naagarik puraskaron main chauthaa sarvocch puraskaar he
